<P style="page-break-before:always; margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt"><B>Item 1.01 &nbsp;Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement.</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:27pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt">As described under Item 2.03 below, on December 29, 2004 the Registrant entered into the Loan Agreement (as defined below). The information regarding the Loan Agreement set forth in Item&nbsp;2.03 is incorporated herein by reference.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt"><B>Item 2.01 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Completion of Acquisition or Disposition of Assets.</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:27pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt">On December 29, 2004, the Registrant, a wholly-owned subsidiary of Loews Corporation, completed its previously announced acquisition (the &quot;Acquisition&quot;) of all of the limited partnership interests of Gulf South Pipeline, L.P. (&quot;Gulf South&quot;) and all of the limited liability company interests of GS Pipeline Company, LLC, the sole general partner of Gulf South, from Entergy-Koch, LP for a purchase price of $1,136,000,000 in cash, subject to adjustment (the &quot;Purchase Price&quot;). Entergy-Koch, LP is a venture of Entergy Corporation and Koch Energy, Inc., a subsidiary of Koch Industries, Inc. </P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:27pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:27pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt">The Registrant funded payment of the Purchase Price and related expenses of the transaction with cash contributed by its parent and the proceeds of a $575 million loan (the &#147;Acquisition Loan&#148;) made by affiliates of Citigroup Global Markets Inc. (&#147;CGMI&#148;) and Lehman Brothers Inc. (&#147;LBI&#148;). </P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt">Gulf South Pipeline owns and operates an 8,000-mile interstate natural gas pipeline, gathering and storage system located in the U.S. Gulf Coast. Gulf South is headquartered in Houston with field offices located in Texas, Louisiana, Mississippi, Alabama and Florida. The Gulf South pipeline system is comprised of approximately 6,800 miles of interstate transmission pipeline, 1,200 miles of gathering pipeline and 68.5 billion cubic feet of working gas storage capacity.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; padding-left:72pt; text-indent:-72pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt"><B>Item 2.03 &nbsp;Creation of a Direct Financial Obligation or an Obligation under an Off-Balance Sheet Arrangement of a Registrant.</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As discussed above under Item 2.01, on December 29, 2004, the Registrant borrowed the Acquisition Loan pursuant to the terms of a 364-Day Term Loan Agreement, dated as of December 29, 2004 (the &#147;Loan Agreement&#148;), among the Registrant, as borrower, the several banks and other financial institutions or entities from time to time party to the Loan Agreement, as lenders, Citicorp North America, Inc., as administrative agent for the Lenders, Lehman Commercial Paper Inc., as syndication agent, and CGMI and LBI as joint lead arrangers and joint book managers. The Acquisition Loan bears interest at a floating rate equal to LIBOR plus an Applicable Margin and matures on December 28, 2005, subject to acceleration by the Lenders upon the occurrence of certain customary Events of Default, all as provided in the Loan Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt"><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Courier New; font-size:11pt"><BR></P>

<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Section 9.4 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Limitations on Liability of Seller &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;38</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Section 9.5 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Waiver of Other Representations. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;40</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Section 9.6 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Purchase Price Adjustment &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;40</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Section 9.7 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Exclusive Remedy &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;40</P>
<P style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=center>ARTICLE X<BR>

<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Section 10.1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Termination &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;41</P>

MISCELLANEOUS</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Section 11.1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Notices &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;42</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Section 11.2 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Assignment &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;43</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Section 11.3 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Rights of Third Parties &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;43</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Section 11.4 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Expenses &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;43</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Section 11.5 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Counterparts &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;43</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt">Section 11.6 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Entire Agreement &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;43</P>

<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>PURCHASE AND SALE AGREEMENT</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>THIS PURCHASE AND SALE AGREEMENT, dated as of November 20, 2004 (this &#147;<B><I>Agreement</I></B>&#148;), is entered into by and between Entergy-Koch, LP, a limited partnership organized under the Laws of Delaware (&#147;<B><I>Seller</I></B>&#148;) and TGT Pipeline, LLC, a limited liability company organized under the Laws of Delaware (&#147;<B><I>Buyer</I></B>&#148;).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B><U>RECITALS</U></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>WHEREAS, Seller owns and desires to sell to Buyer, and Buyer desires to purchase from Seller, on the terms and subject to the conditions set forth herein, (i) 100% of the member interests in GS Pipeline Company, LLC, a limited liability company organized under the Laws of Delaware (&#147;<B><I>GS Pipeline</I></B>&#148;), which is the owner of 100% of the general partner interests in Gulf South Pipeline Company, LP, a limited partnership organized under the Laws of Delaware (&#147;<B><I>Gulf South</I></B>&#148;) and (ii)&nbsp;100% of the limited partner interests in Gulf South (such member interests in GS Pipeline and limited partner interests in Gulf South being collectively the &#147;<B><I>Purchased Interests</I></B>&#148;); and</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>WHEREAS, Gulf South owns and operates the Gulf South Pipeline System which consists of natural gas transportation, gathering and storage facilities in Texas, Louisiana, Mississippi, Alabama and Florida; </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the premises and mutual covenants contained herein and other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and sufficiency of which are hereby acknowledged, the Parties agree as follows:</P>
<A NAME="_Toc75944701"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595051"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595137"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595226"></A><A NAME="_Toc82844748"></A><A NAME="_Toc82856704"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881206"></A><A NAME="_Toc83613001"></A><A NAME="_Toc85445660"></A><A NAME="_Toc85974009"></A><A NAME="_Toc85974322"></A><A NAME="_Toc86037908"></A><A NAME="_Toc86234067"></A><A NAME="_Toc87031618"></A><A NAME="_Toc87106477"></A><A NAME="_Toc87106856"></A><A NAME="_Toc87184044"></A><A NAME="_Toc87365652"></A><A NAME="_Toc87444295"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446014"></A><A NAME="_Toc88122480"></A><A NAME="_Toc88202522"></A><A NAME="_Toc88218649"></A><A NAME="_Toc88219825"></A><A NAME="_Toc88221704"></A><A NAME="_Toc88312782"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314021"></A><A NAME="_Toc88379361"></A><A NAME="_Toc88379454"></A><A NAME="_Toc88470921"></A><A NAME="_Toc88484531"></A><A NAME="_Toc88484624"></A><A NAME="_Toc88547118"></A><A NAME="_Toc88579364"></A><A NAME="_Toc88580507"></A><A NAME="_Toc88711224"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713981"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt
; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>ARTICLE I<BR>
<A NAME="_Toc82881291"></A>DEFINITIONS AND RULES OF CONSTRUCTION</B></P>
<A NAME="_Toc75944703"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595052"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881207"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881292"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446015"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314022"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713982"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 1.1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Definitions</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;As used herein, the following terms shall have the following meanings:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Accountant</I></B>&#148; has the meaning provided such term in Section 2.4(d).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Affiliate</I></B>&#148; means, with respect to any Person, any other Person that, directly or indirectly, controls, is controlled by or is under common control with, such specified Person through one or more intermediaries or otherwise. &nbsp;For the purposes of this definition, &#147;control&#148; means, where used with respect to any Person, the possession, directly or indirectly, of the power to direct or cause the direction of the management and policies of such Person, whether through the ownership of voting securities, by contract or otherwise, and the terms &#147;controlling&#148; and &#147;controlled&#148; have correlative meanings.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Affiliate Employees</I></B>&#148; has the meaning provided such term in Section 6.6(b).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Agreement</I></B>&#148; has the meaning provided such term in the preamble to this Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Balance Sheet Date</I></B>&#148; means September&nbsp;30, 2004.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Bonds</I></B>&#148; means Seller&#146;s 3.65% Senior Notes Due 2006 issued pursuant to Indenture dated August&nbsp;21, 2003 between Seller and La Salle National Bank Association and Seller&#146;s 6.90% Senior Notes Due 2011 issued pursuant to Indenture dated as of July&nbsp;24, 2001 between Seller and La Salle National Bank Association.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Business Day</I></B>&#148; means any day that is not a Saturday, Sunday or legal holiday in the States of New York or Texas or a federal holiday in the United States.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Buyer</I></B>&#148; has the meaning provided such term in the preamble to this Agreement.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Dollars</I></B>&#148; and &#147;<B>$</B>&#148; mean the lawful currency of the United States.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Entergy</I></B>&#148; means Entergy Corporation, a corporation organized under the Laws of Delaware.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Environmental Law</I></B>&#148; means any applicable Law relating to the environment, natural resources, or the protection thereof, including any applicable provisions of the Comprehensive Environmental Response, Compensation and Liability Act, 42 U.S.C. &#167; 9601 <U>et</U> <U>seq.</U>, the Hazardous Materials Transportation Act, 49 U.S.C. &#167; 5101 <U>et</U> <U>seq.</U>, the Resource Conservation and Recovery Act, 42 U.S.C. &#167;&nbsp;6901 <U>et</U> <U>seq.</U>, the Clean Water Act, 33 U.S.C. &#167;&nbsp;1251 <U>et</U> <U>seq.</U>, the Clean Air Act, 42 U.S.C. &#167;&nbsp;7401 <U>et</U> <U>seq.</U>, the Toxic Substances Control Act, 15 U.S.C. &#167;&nbsp;2601 <U>et</U> <U>seq.</U>, the Federal Insecticide, Fungicide, and Rodenticide Act, 7 U.S.C. &#167;&nbsp;136 <U>et</U> <U>seq.</U>, and the Oil Pollution Act of 1990, 33 U.S.C. &#167;&nbsp;2701 <U>et</U> <U>seq.</U>, a
nd all analogous state or local statutes, and the regulations promulgated pursuant thereto.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>ERISA</I></B>&#148; means the Employee Retirement Income Security Act of 1974, as amended.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Estimated Purchase Price</I></B>&#148; means Seller&#146;s good faith estimate of the Purchase Price as set forth in a statement delivered to Buyer at least two Business Days before the Closing.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Financial Statements</I></B>&#148; has the meaning provided such term in Section 4.4.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Governmental Authority</I></B>&#148; means any federal, state, municipal, local, foreign or similar governmental authority, regulatory or administrative agency, court or arbitral body.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>GS Pipeline</I></B>&#148; has the meaning provided such term in the recitals of this Agreement.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>HSR Act</I></B>&#148; means the Hart-Scott-Rodino Antitrust Improvements Act of 1976, as amended.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Indebtedness</I></B>&#148; means for any Person (i) indebtedness for borrowed money, including any obligation to reimburse any bank or other Person in respect of amounts paid or payable under a standby letter of credit; (ii) obligations of such Person to pay the deferred purchase or acquisition price of property or services, other than trade accounts payable arising, and accrued expenses incurred, in the ordinary course of business; (iii) indebtedness for borrowed money of others secured by a Lien on the property of such Person, whether or not the respective indebtedness so secured has been assumed by such Person; (iv) capital lease obligations of such Person or (v) any guarantee with respect to Indebtedness of another Person.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Knowledge</I></B>&#148; as to Buyer means the actual knowledge of those persons listed in <U>Schedule&nbsp;1.1(a)</U> and as to Seller means the actual knowledge of those persons listed in <U>Schedule&nbsp;1.1(b)</U>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Koch</I></B>&#148; means Koch Industries, Inc., a corporation organized under the Laws of Kansas.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Law</I></B>&#148; means any applicable law, rule, regulation, ordinance, order, judgment or decree of a Governmental Authority, in each case as in effect on and as interpreted on the date of this Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Lien(s)</I></B>&#148; means any charges, pledges, options, mortgages, deeds of trust, hypothecations, security interests or other encumbrances.</P>

<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Losses</I></B>&#148; means all claims, liabilities, losses, damages, fines, penalties, judgments, settlements, awards, costs and expenses (including reasonable fees and expenses of counsel, consultants, experts and other professional fees and any and all costs and expenses (including reasonable legal fees and accounting fees) incident to the enforcement of the indemnification provisions of this Agreement); <I>provided, however, </I>that Losses shall not include any special, punitive, exemplary, incidental, consequential or indirect damages or any lost profits, lost benefits, loss of enterprise value, diminution in value of any business, damage to reputation or loss to goodwill; <I>provided</I>, further, however, that the preceding proviso shall not apply to the extent a Party is required to pay such damages to a third party in connection with a matte
r for which such Party is entitled to indemnification under Article IX.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Material Adverse Effect</I></B>&#148; means, with respect to any Person, any circumstance, change or effect that (i) is materially adverse to the business, operations (including results of operation), assets, liabilities or financial condition of such Person (and in the case of either Company, of the Companies taken as a whole) or (ii)&nbsp;materially impedes the ability of such Person to complete the transactions contemplated herein or to perform its obligations hereunder, but in the case of clause (i) above, shall exclude any circumstance, change or effect resulting or arising from: </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;any change in general economic conditions in the industries or markets in which either of the Companies operate;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;seasonal reductions in revenues and/or earnings of the Companies in the ordinary course of their respective businesses;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;national or international political conditions, including any engagement in hostilities, whether or not pursuant to the declaration of a national emergency or war, or the occurrence of any military or terrorist attack; </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(d) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;changes in Law or GAAP; </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(e) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the entry into or announcement of this Agreement, actions contemplated by this Agreement, or the consummation of the transactions contemplated hereby; </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(f) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;matters that will be reflected in the determination of the Net Working Capital as of the Closing Date; and</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(g) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;the loss of any employee of Gulf South or any Affiliate Employee.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Any determination as to whether any circumstance, change or effect has a Material Adverse Effect shall be made only after taking into account all effective insurance coverages, third-party indemnifications and Tax Benefits with respect to such circumstance, change or effect.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Material Contracts</I></B>&#148; has the meaning provided such term in Section 4.6(a).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>NGA</I></B>&#148; has the meaning provided such term in Section 4.18.</P>

<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Net Working Capital</I></B>&#148;, which may be positive or negative, means an amount equal to (1) the total current assets of the Companies minus (2) the total current liabilities of the Companies, determined in accordance with GAAP on a basis consistent with past practice (without regard to Buyer&#146;s purchase accounting adjustments) minus (3) the sum of (A) $5,400,000 and (B) any other amounts received by Gulf South on or prior to the Closing Date pursuant to Section&nbsp;7 of the Termination and Release Agreement dated November&nbsp;16, 2004 between Reiss Remediation Inc. and Gulf South to the extent that Gulf South has not either (x) paid any such amounts for the environmental insurance policy described in such Section&nbsp;7 and not included any such amounts as a prepaid insurance current asset in the calculation of Net Working Capital as of 
the Closing or (y) incurred a liability for such policy which is included as a current liability in the calculation of the Net Working Capital as of the Closing; <I>provided, however, </I>that the following items shall be excluded from the calculation of Net Working Capital: (i) Excluded Assets; (ii) assets such as prepaid insurance which will be extinguished in connection with the transactions contemplated hereby, if any, to the extent that neither Company is entitled to any refund relating thereto; (iii)&nbsp;intercompany Indebtedness distributed or cancelled pursuant to Section 6.9 hereof; (iv) any reversal of current liability reserves or reversals of current asset reserves, including contra-assets accounts for current assets (including allowances for doubtful accounts) and (v)&nbsp;any changes to current assets and liabilities resulting from a reclassification of any non-current assets and liabilities. &nbsp;For illustrative purposes only, the components of Net Working Capital as of the Balance Sheet Da
te are shown on <U>Schedule 1.1(f)</U>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Non-Transferred Employees</I></B>&#148; has the meaning provided such term in Section 6.6(f).</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Parties</I></B>&#148; means Seller and Buyer.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&#147;<B><I>Permitted Liens</I></B>&#148; means (i) Liens for Taxes, impositions, assessments, fees, rents or other governmental charges levied or assessed or imposed not yet delinquent or being contested in good faith by appropriate proceedings, (ii) statutory Liens (including materialmen&#146;s, warehousemen&#146;s, mechanic&#146;s, repairmen&#146;s, landlord&#146;s, and other similar Liens) arising in the ordinary course of business securing payments not yet delinquent or being contested in good faith by appropriate proceedings, (iii) Liens of public record which would not reasonably be expected to result in a Material Adverse Effect on the Companies, (iv) the rights of lessors and lessees under leases executed in the ordinary course of business, (v) the rights of licensors and licensees under licenses executed in the ordinary course of business, (vi) restrictive covenants, easements 
and defects, imperfections or irregularities of title or Liens, if any, as would not reasonably be expected to result in a Material Adverse Effect on the Companies, (vii) purchase money Liens and Liens securing rental payments under capital lease arrangements executed in </P>

<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>the ordinary course of business, (viii) preferential purchase rights and other similar arrangements with respect to which consents or waivers are obtained for this transaction or as to which the time for asserting such rights has expired at the Closing Date without an exercise of such rights, (ix)&nbsp;restrictions on transfer with respect to which consents or waivers are obtained for this transaction, (x) any Liens created pursuant to operating or similar agreements executed in the ordinary course of business, (xi) Liens entered into in the ordinary course of business which do not secure the payment of Indebtedness for Borrowed Money and which do not materially and adversely affect the ability of the Companies to conduct their business, (xii)&nbsp;Liens referenced in any real property files made available by Seller to Buyer or in the Disclosure Schedules which

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If a term is defined as one part of speech (such as a noun), it shall have a corresponding meaning when used as another part of speech (such as a verb). &nbsp;Terms defined in the singular have the corresponding meanings in the plural, and vice versa. &nbsp;Unless the context of this Agreement clearly requires otherwise, words importing the masculine gender shall include the feminine and neutral genders and vice versa. The term &#147;includes&#148; or &#147;including&#148; shall mean &#147;including without limitation.&#148; &nbsp;The words &#147;hereof,&#148; &#147;hereto,&#148; &#147;hereby,&#148; &#147;herein,&#148; &#147;hereunder&#148; and words of similar import, when used in this Agreement, shall refer to this Agreement as a whole and not to any particular section or article in which such words appear. &nbsp;The phrase &#147;ordinary c
ourse of business&#148; shall mean, with respect to the subject Person, the ordinary course of business consistent with past practice.</P>

PURCHASE AND SALE; CLOSING<A NAME="_Toc82881294"></A></B></P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595055"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881210"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881295"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446018"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314025"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944709"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713985"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 2.1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Purchase and Sale of Purchased Interests</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;At the Closing, upon the terms and subject to the conditions set forth in this Agreement, Seller shall sell, assign, transfer and convey to Buyer, and Buyer shall purchase and acquire from Seller, the Purchased Interests, free and clear of any Liens other than transfer restrictions imposed thereon by applicable securities Laws.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82881211"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881296"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446019"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314026"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944711"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595056"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713986"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 2.2 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Purchase Price</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;The aggregate consideration payable by Buyer to Seller for the Purchased Interests (the &#147;<B><I>Purchase Price</I></B>&#148;) shall consist of $1,136,000,000 (the &#147;<B><I>Base Purchase Price</I></B>&#148;) plus the Net Working Capital as of the Closing Date.<A NAME="_Toc75944715"></A></P>
<A NAME="_Toc87446020"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314027"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713987"></A><BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 2.3 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>The Closing.</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The closing of the transactions contemplated by this Agreement (the &#147;<B><I>Closing</I></B>&#148;) shall take place at the offices of Vinson &amp; Elkins L.L.P., 1001 Fannin, Houston, Texas 77002, commencing at 10:00 a.m. local time on the third Business Day following the satisfaction or waiver of all conditions to the obligations of the Parties to consummate the transactions contemplated hereby (other than conditions with respect to actions the Parties shall take at the Closing itself) or such other date as Buyer and Seller may mutually determine (the &#147;<B><I>Closing Date</I></B>&#148;). &nbsp;The Closing shall be deemed to have been consummated at 9:00 a.m. Houston time on the Closing Date.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;At the Closing, Seller will deliver the following documents and deliverables to Buyer:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(i) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;An Assignment and Assumption Agreement in the form of Exhibit 2.3(b)(i) effecting the transfer to Buyer of ownership of all of the Purchased Interests;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(ii) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A Parent Tax Indemnity Agreement in the form of Exhibit&nbsp;2.3(b)(ii) from Koch;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(iii) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A certificate certifying that the transactions contemplated hereby are exempt from withholding under Section 1445 of the Code;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(iv) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The resignations (or evidence of removal) of each officer or director of the Companies, effective as of the Closing, for which Buyer has requested a resignation at least five Business Days prior to the Closing; </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(v) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A Parent Guaranty in the form of Exhibit 2.3(b)(v) executed by each of the Parent Companies; and </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(vi) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Such other certificates, instruments of conveyance, and documents as may be reasonably requested by Buyer and agreed to by Seller prior to the Closing Date to carry out the intent and purposes of this Agreement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;At the Closing, Buyer will deliver the following documents and deliverables to Seller:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(i) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;An Assignment and Assumption Agreement in the form of Exhibit&nbsp;2.3(b)(i) effecting the transfer to Buyer of ownership of all of the Purchased Interests;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(ii) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;An amount equal to the Estimated Purchase Price by wire transfer of immediately available funds to an account or accounts specified by Seller; </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(iii) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A Release Agreement in the form attached as Exhibit 2.3(c)(iii); and</P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(iv) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Such other certificates, instruments, and documents as may be reasonably requested by Seller and agreed to by Buyer prior to the Closing Date to carry out the intent and purposes of this Agreement.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc87446021"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314028"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944717"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595058"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881213"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881298"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713988"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 2.4 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Post-Closing Purchase Price Reconciliation.</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As soon as reasonably practicable following the Closing Date, and in any event within 60 days thereafter, Buyer shall prepare and deliver to Seller a calculation of Net Working Capital as of the Closing, together with reasonably detailed supporting information (the &#147;<B><I>Closing Statement</I></B>&#148;).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;From and after the delivery of the Closing Statement, Buyer shall provide Seller and its Representatives reasonable access to the records and employees of the Companies and shall cause the employees of the Companies to cooperate in all reasonable respects with Seller in connection with its review of such work papers and other documents and information relating to the calculation of Net Working Capital as of the Closing as Seller shall reasonably request and that are available to Buyer, the Companies or the Companies&#146; independent public accountants.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Within 45 days after Seller&#146;s receipt of the Closing Statement, Seller shall notify Buyer as to whether Seller agrees or disagrees with the Closing Statement and, if Seller disagrees, such notice shall set forth in reasonable detail the particulars of such disagreement. &nbsp;If Seller provides a notice of agreement or does not provide a notice of disagreement within such 45 day period, then Seller shall be deemed to have accepted the calculations and the amounts set forth in the Closing Statement delivered by Buyer, which shall then be final, binding and conclusive for all purposes hereunder. &nbsp;If any such notice of disagreement is timely provided, then Buyer and Seller shall each use Reasonable Efforts for a period of 30 days thereafter to resolve any disagreements with respect to the calculations in the Closing Statement.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(d) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If, at the end of the 30-day resolution period, the Parties are unable to resolve any disagreements as to items in the Closing Statement, then KPMG LLP (or such other independent accounting firm of recognized national standing as may be mutually selected by Buyer and Seller) shall resolve any remaining disagreements. &nbsp;If KPMG LLP is unwilling or unable to serve in such capacity then PricewaterhouseCoopers U.S. shall be engaged to serve in such capacity. &nbsp;If PricewaterhouseCoopers U.S. is not willing or able to serve in such capacity, then Seller shall within 10 days deliver to Buyer a listing of three other accounting firms of recognized national or regional standing and Buyer shall within 10 days after receipt of such list, select one of such three accounting firms (such firm as is ultimately selected pursuant to the aforementioned
 procedures being the &#147;<B><I>Accountant</I></B>&#148;). &nbsp;The Accountant shall be charged with determining as promptly as practicable, but in any event within 30 days after the date on which such dispute is referred to the Accountant any disputed items required to determine the Net Working Capital as of the Closing. &nbsp;The costs and expenses of the Accountant shall be borne 50% by Seller and 50% by Buyer. &nbsp;The determination of the Accountant shall be final, binding and conclusive for all purposes hereunder. &nbsp;Such amounts as finally determined by the Accountant shall be used to determine the Purchase Price.</P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(e) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Within five Business Days of the date on which the last disputed item required to determine the Net Working Capital as of the Closing is resolved pursuant to this Section 2.4, Buyer shall pay to Seller an amount equal to the excess, if any, of the Purchase Price minus the Estimated Purchase Price, or Seller shall pay to Buyer an amount equal to the excess, if any, of the Estimated Purchase Price minus the Purchase Price, in each case together with interest at a rate equal to 5% per annum on such excess from the Closing Date to the date of payment.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595064"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595150"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595239"></A><A NAME="_Toc82844761"></A><A NAME="_Toc82856717"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881218"></A><A NAME="_Toc83613009"></A><A NAME="_Toc85445668"></A><A NAME="_Toc85974017"></A><A NAME="_Toc85974330"></A><A NAME="_Toc86037916"></A><A NAME="_Toc86234075"></A><A NAME="_Toc87031627"></A><A NAME="_Toc87106485"></A><A NAME="_Toc87106864"></A><A NAME="_Toc87184052"></A><A NAME="_Toc87365660"></A><A NAME="_Toc87444303"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446022"></A><A NAME="_Toc88122488"></A><A NAME="_Toc88202530"></A><A NAME="_Toc88218657"></A><A NAME="_Toc88219833"></A><A NAME="_Toc88221712"></A><A NAME="_Toc88312790"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314029"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944721"></A><A NAME="_Toc88379369"></A><A NAME="_Toc88379462"></A><A NAME="_Toc88470929"></A><A NAME="_Toc88484539"></A><A NAME="_Toc88484632"></A><A NAME="_Toc88547126"></A><A NAME="_Toc88579372"></A><A NAME="_Toc88580515"></A><A NAME="_Toc88711232"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713989"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt
; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>ARTICLE III<BR>
REPRESENTATIONS AND WARRANTIES RELATING TO SELLER<A NAME="_Toc82881303"></A></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Seller hereby represents and warrants to Buyer as follows:</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595065"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881219"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881304"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446023"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314030"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713990"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 3.1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Organization of Seller</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Seller is a limited partnership, duly organized, validly existing and in good standing under the Laws of the State of Delaware. &nbsp;</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595066"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881220"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881305"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446024"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314031"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944723"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713991"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 3.2 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Authorization; Enforceability<A NAME="_Toc82595067"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881221"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881306"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944725"></A></I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Seller has all requisite partnership power and authority to execute and deliver this Agreement and to perform all obligations to be performed by it hereunder. &nbsp;The execution and delivery of this Agreement and the consummation of the transactions contemplated hereby have been duly and validly authorized and approved by all requisite partnership action on the part of Seller. &nbsp;This Agreement has been duly and validly executed and delivered by Seller, and this Agreement constitutes a valid and binding obligation of Seller, enforceable against Seller in accordance with its terms, subject to applicable bankruptcy, insolvency, fraudulent conveyance, reorganization, moratorium and similar Laws affecting creditors&#146; rights generally and subject, as to enforceability, to general principles of equity.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc87446025"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314032"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713992"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 3.3 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>No Conflict</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;The execution and delivery of this Agreement by Seller and the consummation of the transactions contemplated hereby by Seller (assuming all filings, consents, approvals, authorizations and notices set forth in <U>Schedule 3.3</U> (collectively, the &#147;<B><I>Seller Approvals</I></B>&#148;) have been made, given or obtained) do not and shall not:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;violate any Law applicable to Seller or require any filing with, consent, approval or authorization of, or notice to, any Governmental Authority or any other Person;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;violate any Organizational Document of Seller; or</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(i) breach or conflict with any Contract to which Seller is a party or by which Seller may be bound, (ii) result in the termination of any such Contract, (iii) result in the creation of any Lien upon any of the Purchased Interests or (iv) constitute an event which, after notice or lapse of time or both, would result in any such breach, termination or creation of a Lien upon any of the Purchased Interests;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>except, in the case of clause (a) and (c) above, as would not reasonably be expected, either individually or in the aggregate, to have a Material Adverse Effect on the ability of Seller to enter into and timely perform its obligations under this Agreement and the other agreements contemplated hereby to be executed by Seller.</P>

<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 3.4 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Litigation</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Except as set forth on <U>Schedule 4.8</U>, as of the date of this Agreement, (a)&nbsp;there are no lawsuits or actions before any Governmental Authority pending or, to the Knowledge of Seller, threatened in writing against Seller, Entergy, Koch or their Affiliates that would reasonably be expected to have a Material Adverse Effect on the assets of the Companies or the ability of Seller to perform its obligations under this Agreement and (b)&nbsp;there are no orders or unsatisfied judgments from any Governmental Authority binding upon Seller, Entergy, Koch or their Affiliates that would reasonably be expected to have a Material Adverse Effect on the assets of the Companies or the ability of Seller to perform its obligations under this Agreement.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595069"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881223"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881308"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446027"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314034"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944729"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595068"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881222"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881307"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944727"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713994"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 3.5 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Brokers&#146; Fees</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Except for Lehman Brothers, Inc., no broker, finder, investment banker or other Person is entitled to any brokerage fee, finders&#146; fee or other commission in connection with the transactions contemplated by this Agreement based upon arrangements made by Seller or any of its Affiliates.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc87446028"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314035"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713995"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 3.6 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Ownership of Purchased Interests.</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Seller has good title to, holds of record and owns beneficially the Purchased Interests free and clear of any Liens other than transfer restrictions imposed thereon by applicable securities Laws and Permitted Liens. &nbsp;All of the Purchased Interests are held by Seller, and the Purchased Interests represent, directly or indirectly, 100% of the outstanding equity interests in the Companies. &nbsp;On the Closing Date, upon payment of the Purchase Price in accordance with Section 2.3, the Purchased Interests will be acquired by Buyer free and clear of all Liens (other than restrictions imposed thereon by applicable securities Laws). </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;GS Pipeline has good title to, holds of record and owns beneficially all of the general partner interests in Gulf South free and clear of any Liens other than transfer restrictions imposed thereon by applicable securities Laws and, prior to Closing, Permitted Liens.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc75944731"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595070"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595156"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595245"></A><A NAME="_Toc82844767"></A><A NAME="_Toc82856723"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881224"></A><A NAME="_Toc85445675"></A><A NAME="_Toc85974024"></A><A NAME="_Toc85974337"></A><A NAME="_Toc86037923"></A><A NAME="_Toc86234082"></A><A NAME="_Toc87031634"></A><A NAME="_Toc87106492"></A><A NAME="_Toc87106871"></A><A NAME="_Toc87184059"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;There are no outstanding options, warrants, rights or other securities convertible into or exchangeable or exercisable for equity securities, any other commitments or agreements providing for the issuance of additional equity interests or the repurchase or redemption of equity interests, and there are no agreements of any kind which may obligate either of the Companies to issue, purchase, redeem or otherwise acquire an
y of their respective equity interests. &nbsp;There are no voting agreements, proxies or other similar agreements or understandings with respect to the equity interests of either Company.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc87365667"></A><A NAME="_Toc87444310"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446029"></A><A NAME="_Toc88122495"></A><A NAME="_Toc88202537"></A><A NAME="_Toc88218664"></A><A NAME="_Toc88219840"></A><A NAME="_Toc88221719"></A><A NAME="_Toc88312797"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314036"></A><A NAME="_Toc88379376"></A><A NAME="_Toc88379469"></A><A NAME="_Toc88470936"></A><A NAME="_Toc88484546"></A><A NAME="_Toc88484639"></A><A NAME="_Toc88547133"></A><A NAME="_Toc88579379"></A><A NAME="_Toc88580522"></A><A NAME="_Toc88711239"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713996"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>ARTICLE IV<BR>
REPRESENTATIONS AND WARRANTIES RELATING TO THE COMPANIES<A NAME="_Toc82881309"></A></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Seller hereby represents and warrants to Buyer as follows:</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595071"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881225"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881310"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446030"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314037"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944733"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713997"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 4.1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Organization of the Companies</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Each of the Companies is duly organized, validly existing and in good standing under the Laws of the jurisdiction of its organization and has the requisite limited liability company or partnership power and authority to own or lease its assets and to conduct its business as it is now being conducted. &nbsp;Each of the Companies is duly licensed or qualified in each jurisdiction in which the ownership or operation </P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>of its assets or the character of its activities is such as to require it to be so licensed or qualified, except where the failure to be so licensed or qualified would not reasonably be expected to have a Material Adverse Effect on the Companies. &nbsp;Seller has made available to Buyer true copies of all existing Organizational Documents of the Companies.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595073"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881227"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881312"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446031"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314038"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944737"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713998"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 4.2 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>No Conflict</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;The execution and delivery of this Agreement by Seller and the consummation of the transactions contemplated hereby by Seller (assuming all of the Seller Approvals have been made, given or obtained) do not and shall not:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;violate any Law applicable to the Companies or require any filing with, consent, approval or authorization of, or notice to, any Governmental Authority or any other Person;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;violate any Organizational Document of the Companies; or</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(i) breach or conflict with any Contract or Permit of the Companies, (ii) result in the termination of any such Contract or Permit of the Companies, (iii)&nbsp;result in the creation of any Lien under any Contract or on any assets of the Companies or (iv)&nbsp;constitute an event which, after notice or lapse of time or both, would result in any such breach, termination or creation of a Lien or would create in any party the right to accelerate, terminate, modify, or cancel a Contract or Permit of the Companies;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>except, in the case of clause (a) and (c) above, as would not reasonably be expected, either individually or in the aggregate, to have a Material Adverse Effect on the Companies or on the ability of Seller to enter into and timely perform its obligations under this Agreement and the other agreements contemplated hereby to be executed by Seller.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc87446032"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314039"></A><A NAME="_Toc88713999"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 4.3 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Subsidiaries</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Except for the 1% general partner interest that GS Pipeline owns in Gulf South, neither of the Companies owns any equity interests in any Person.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595074"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881228"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881313"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446033"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314040"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944739"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714000"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 4.4 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Financial Statements</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;<U>Schedule 4.4</U> sets forth true and complete copies of the following financial statements (collectively, the &#147;<B><I>Financial Statements</I></B>&#148;): (i)&nbsp;the audited balance sheet of Gulf South (with related statements of income and comprehensive income, changes in partners&#146; capital and cash flows) as of, and for the year ended, December 31, 2003, (ii)&nbsp;the unaudited balance sheet of GS Pipeline (with related statements of income and comprehensive income, changes in member&#146;s capital and cash flows) as of, and for the year ended, December 31, 2003, (iii)&nbsp;the unaudited balance sheet of Gulf South (with related statements of income and comprehensive income, changes in partners&#146; capital and cash flows) as of, and for the year-to-date ended on, the Balance Sheet Date and (iv)&nbsp;the unaudited balance sheet of GS Pipeline (with related statements of income and 
comprehensive income, changes in member&#146;s capital and cash flows) as of, and for the year-to-date ended on, the Balance Sheet Date. &nbsp;The Financial Statements have been prepared in accordance with GAAP (except as otherwise stated in the footnotes or the audit opinion related thereto), and present fairly in accordance with GAAP, in all material respects, the financial position and the results of operations of the Companies as of, and for the periods ended on, such dates, except for the absence of footnotes with respect to the Financial Statements described in clauses (ii), (iii) and </P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(iv) and except for normal year end adjustments with respect to the Financial Statements described in clauses (iii) and (iv). </P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595075"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881229"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881314"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446034"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314041"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944741"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714001"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 4.5 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Absence of Certain Changes</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Except as disclosed on <U>Schedule 4.5</U>, from the Balance Sheet Date until the date of this Agreement, (a) there has not been any Material Adverse Effect on the Companies and (b) the business of each of the Companies has been conducted, in all material respects, only in the ordinary course of business. &nbsp;Without limiting the generality of the foregoing, to the Knowledge of Seller and except as set forth on <U>Schedule 4.5</U>, since the Balance Sheet Date until the date of this Agreement, the Companies have not taken any of the actions described in Section 6.1(b).</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595076"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881230"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881315"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446035"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314042"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714002"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 4.6 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Contracts.</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><U>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Schedule 4.6(a)</U> contains a true and complete listing of the following Contracts (other than Contracts that contain confidentiality provisions prohibiting their disclosure) to which either of the Companies is a party in effect on the date of this Agreement (each Contract that is required to be listed on <U>Schedule 4.6(a)</U>, together with any other Contract that Seller would have been required to disclose on <U>Schedule 4.6(a)</U> but for the fact that they contain confidentiality provisions prohibiting such disclosure, being &#147;<B><I>Material Contracts</I></B>&#148;):</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(i) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;except for any intercompany indebtedness that will be cancelled prior to Closing, each Contract for Indebtedness for borrowed money involving an obligation in excess of $100,000 and each Contract for other Indebtedness involving an obligation in excess of $1,000,000;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(ii) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;each natural gas transportation Contract and storage Contract that individually involves revenues of the Company in excess of $450,000 for the year-to-date period ended on the Balance Sheet Date, all of which listed natural gas transportation and storage Contracts represent in the aggregate in excess of 80% of the total revenues of the Companies for the year-to-date period ending on the Balance Sheet Date;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(iii) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;each Contract involving a remaining commitment by a Company to pay capital expenditures with respect to its business in excess of $1,000,000;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(iv) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;each Contract for lease of personal property or real property involving aggregate payments in excess of $500,000 in any calendar year;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(v) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;each employment Contract involving aggregate payments in excess of $100,000 in any calendar year, and each Contract providing retention, severance or project bonus payments in excess of $50,000 individually or $200,000 in the aggregate, in each case that have not been paid in full as of the date of this Agreement;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(vi) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;each Contract providing for any compensation payable as a result of the consummation of the transaction contemplated by this Agreement in excess of $50,000 individually or $200,000 in the aggregate;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(vii) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;except for Contracts of the nature described in clause&nbsp;(ii) above, each Contract between Seller or a Seller Affiliate (other than either of the Companies) on the one </P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>hand, and either of the Companies, on the other hand, identifying those Contracts that will survive the Closing (with specific reference to those which cannot be cancelled by a Company upon 30 days or less notice without payment penalty) and those that will terminate on or prior to the Closing;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(viii) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;each Contract that provides for a limit on the ability of a Company to compete in any line of business or with any Person or in any geographic area during any period of time after the Closing; and</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:108pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(ix) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;except for Contracts of the nature described in clauses (i) through (viii) above, each Contract involving aggregate payments by or to a Company in excess of $1,000,000 in any future calendar year that cannot be terminated by a Company upon 60&nbsp;days or less notice without payment penalty in excess of $100,000.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;True and complete copies of all Material Contracts (other than any Material Contracts that contain confidentiality provisions prohibiting their disclosure), including all amendments thereto, have been made available to Buyer.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><U>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Schedule 1.1(d)</U> contains a true and complete listing of all material Drop-Down Contracts. &nbsp;<U>Schedule 1.1(e)</U> contains a true and complete listing of all material Shared Contracts. &nbsp;<U>Schedule 6.8</U> contains a true and complete listing of all<B> </B>material Company Guarantees.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(d) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Except as set forth in bullet point 1 on <U>Schedule 4.6(d)</U>, each Material Contract (other than such Material Contracts with respect to which all performance and payment obligations have been fully performed or otherwise discharged by all parties thereto prior to the Closing), Drop-Down Contract, Shared Contract and Company Guarantee (i) is in full force and effect and (ii)&nbsp;represents the legal, valid and binding obligation of the Company, Seller and/or Seller Affiliate that is party thereto and, to the Knowledge of Seller, represents the legal, valid and binding obligation of the other parties thereto, in each case enforceable in accordance with its terms. &nbsp;Except as set forth in <U>Schedule 4.6(d)</U>, (i)&nbsp;neither of the Companies, Seller or Seller Affiliates and, to the Knowledge of Seller, no other party is in material 
breach of any Material Contract, Drop-Down Contract, Shared Contract or Company Guarantee, (ii)&nbsp;neither Seller nor either of the Companies has received any written or, to the Knowledge of Seller, oral notice of termination or breach of any Material Contract, Drop-Down Contract, Shared Contract or Company Guarantee.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595077"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881231"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881316"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446036"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314043"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714003"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 4.7 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Intellectual Property</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;<U>Schedule 4.7</U> sets forth a true and complete list of all material registered Intellectual Property owned by the Companies in connection with their business. &nbsp;Except as set forth on <U>Schedule 4.7</U> and to the Knowledge of Seller, (a) the Companies own or have the right to use pursuant to license, sublicense, agreement or otherwise all material items of Intellectual Property required in the operation of the business of the Companies as presently conducted, (b) no third party has asserted in writing that either Company is infringing the Intellectual Property of such third party or has challenged or questioned the validity or effectiveness of the Companies&#146; rights to their owned Intellectual Property and (c) no third party is infringing the Intellectual Property owned by either of the Companies.</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Except as set forth in <U>Schedule 4.8</U>, as of the date of this Agreement, i) there are no lawsuits or actions before any Governmental Authority pending or, to the Knowledge of Seller, threatened in writing by any Person against either of the Companies that involve claims in excess of $1,000,000 or that would otherwise reasonably be expected to have a Material Adverse Effect on the Companies and ii) to the Knowledge of Seller, there is no injunction, order or unsatisfied judgment from any Governmental Authority that requires payments in excess of $1,000,000 or that would otherwise reasonably be expected to have a Material Adverse Effect on the Companies.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc87446038"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314045"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944753"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595079"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881233"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881318"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714005"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 4.9 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Employee Benefit Plans</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><U>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Schedule 4.9(a)</U> contains a complete list, as of the date of this Agreement, of each material Seller Plan that covers one or more employees of either of the Companies or Affiliate Employees. &nbsp;On or before the date of this Agreement, Seller has made available to Buyer a copy of each Seller Plan listed on <U>Schedule 4.9(a)</U>. &nbsp;As of the date of this Agreement, there are no Company Plans. &nbsp;Neither of the Companies contributes to, or has an obligation to contribute to, any plan subject to Title IV of ERISA.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;With respect to any &#147;employee benefit plan,&#148; within the meaning of Section 3(3) of ERISA, that is a Seller Plan (i) no withdrawal liability, within the meaning of Section 4201 of ERISA, has been incurred by Seller or by any trade or business, whether or not incorporated, that together with Seller would be a &#147;single employer&#148; within the meaning of Section 4001(b) of ERISA (a &#147;<B><I>Commonly Controlled Entity</I></B>&#148;), which withdrawal liability has not been satisfied, (ii) no liability to the Pension Benefit Guaranty Corporation has been incurred by Seller or by any Commonly Controlled Entity, which liability has not been satisfied, (iii) no accumulated funding deficiency, whether or not waived, within the meaning of Section 302 of ERISA or Section 412 of the Code currently exists and (iv) all contributions (incl
uding installments) to such plan required of Seller or any Commonly Controlled Entity by Section 302 of ERISA and Section 412 of the Code have been made.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82881236"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881321"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446039"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314046"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714006"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 4.10 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Taxes</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Except as set forth on <U>Schedule 4.10</U> or as would not reasonably be expected to have a Material Adverse Effect on the Companies, (a) &nbsp;all Tax Returns required to be filed by the Companies have been duly and timely filed with the appropriate Tax Authority, (b) all Taxes for which a Company is liable have been timely paid in full, (c) there are no Liens on any of the assets of the Companies that arose in connection with any failure (or alleged failure) to pay any Tax, (d) there is no claim pending by any applicable Tax Authority in connection with any Tax for which a Company is liable, (e)&nbsp;none of such Tax Returns are now under audit or examination by any Tax Authority, (f) there are no agreements or waivers with respect to a Company providing for an extension of time with respect to the filing of any Tax Returns or the assessment or collection of any Tax, (g) no written claim has be
en made by any Tax Authority in a jurisdiction where a Company does not file a Tax Return that it is or may be subject to taxation in that jurisdiction, (h) neither of the Companies is a party to any Tax allocation or sharing arrangement and (i) since February 1, 2001, each of the Companies has been disregarded as an entity separate from the Seller for federal income tax purposes pursuant to Treasury Regulation Section 301.7701-3(b)(1).</P>

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Except as set forth on <U>Schedule&nbsp;4.11</U> or as would not reasonably be expected to have a Material Adverse Effect on the Companies:</P>
