Buyer and the Companies are indemnified by Koch pursuant to the Parent Tax Indemnity Agreement required under Section 2.3(b)(ii). &nbsp;Buyer shall be solely liable for, shall pay and shall protect, defend, indemnify and hold harmless Seller from any and all Taxes which relate to or result from the income, business, property, status or operations of the Companies after the Closing.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If any claim (an &#147;<B><I>Indemnified Tax Claim</I></B>&#148;) is made by any Tax Authority that, if successful, would result in indemnification of any Party (the &#147;<B><I>Tax Indemnified Party</I></B>&#148;) by another Party (the &#147;<B><I>Tax Indemnifying Party</I></B>&#148;) under this Section 7.3, the Tax Indemnified Party shall promptly, but in no event later than the earlier of (i) 45 days after receipt of notice from the Tax Authority of such claim or (ii) 15 days prior to the date required for the filing of any protest of such claim, notify the Tax Indemnifying Party in writing of such fact; <I>provided, however, </I>that the failure of the Tax Indemnified Party to so notify the Tax Indemnifying Party shall not relieve the Tax Indemnifying Party of its obligations hereunder, unless and only to the extent that such failure to n
otify prejudices the Tax Indemnifying Party.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Tax Indemnifying Party shall control all decisions with respect to any Tax Proceeding involving an Indemnified Tax Claim and the Tax Indemnified Party shall take such action (including settlement with respect to such Tax Proceeding or the prosecution of such Tax Proceeding to a determination in a court or other tribunal of initial or appellate jurisdiction) in connection with a Tax Proceeding involving an Indemnified Tax Claim as the Tax Indemnifying Party shall reasonably request in writing from time to time, including with respect to the selection of counsel and experts and the execution of powers of attorney; <I>provided</I> that (i) within 30 days after the notice required by Section 7.3(b) has been delivered (or such earlier date that any payment of Taxes with respect to such claim is due but in no event sooner than five days after t
he Tax Indemnifying Party&#146;s receipt of such notice), the Tax Indemnifying Party requests </P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>that such claim be contested and (ii) if the Tax Indemnified Party is requested by the Tax Indemnifying Party to pay the Tax claimed and sue for a refund, the Tax Indemnifying Party shall have advanced to the Tax Indemnified Party, on an interest-free basis, the amount of such claim. &nbsp;The Tax Indemnified Party shall not make any payment of an Indemnified Tax Claim for at least 30 days (or such shorter period as may be required by applicable law) after the giving of the notice required by Section 7.3(b) with respect to such claim, shall give to the Tax Indemnifying Party any information requested related to such claim, and otherwise shall cooperate with the Tax Indemnifying Party in order to contest effectively any such claim. &nbsp;Notwithstanding the foregoing, the Parties shall jointly control all decisions with respect to any Tax Proceeding which, in the
 event of an adverse determination, may result in each Party having responsibility for an amount of Taxes hereunder.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(d) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;No claim for indemnity for any Losses or Taxes relating to any single Tax Return or any single item or group of related items shall be permitted pursuant to this Section 7.3 if such claim is for less than $10,000; <I>provided</I> that this limitation shall not apply with respect to any knowing breach by Seller of its representations or covenants in this Agreement.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82881264"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881349"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446078"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314084"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714044"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 7.4 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Scope</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Notwithstanding anything to the contrary herein, this Article VII (and the Parent Tax Indemnity Agreement required under Section 2.3(b)(ii)) shall be the exclusive remedy for any claims relating to Taxes (including any claims relating to representations respecting Tax matters including Section 4.10). &nbsp;The rights hereunder relating to non-income Taxes shall survive the Closing until twelve months after the Closing, and the rights hereunder relating to income<FONT COLOR=#0000FF> </FONT>Taxes shall survive the Closing until 30 days after the expiration of the statute of limitations (including extensions) applicable to such Tax matter. &nbsp;No claim may be made or brought by any Party hereto after the expiration of the applicable survival period unless such claim has been asserted by written notice specifying the details supporting the claim on or prior to the expiration of the applicable surviv
al period.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc75944837"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595111"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595197"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595286"></A><A NAME="_Toc82844808"></A><A NAME="_Toc82856764"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881265"></A><A NAME="_Toc83613059"></A><A NAME="_Toc85445719"></A><A NAME="_Toc85974068"></A><A NAME="_Toc85974381"></A><A NAME="_Toc86037967"></A><A NAME="_Toc86234126"></A><A NAME="_Toc87031683"></A><A NAME="_Toc87106540"></A><A NAME="_Toc87106919"></A><A NAME="_Toc87184107"></A><A NAME="_Toc87365717"></A><A NAME="_Toc87444360"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446079"></A><A NAME="_Toc88122545"></A><A NAME="_Toc88202585"></A><A NAME="_Toc88218712"></A><A NAME="_Toc88219888"></A><A NAME="_Toc88221767"></A><A NAME="_Toc88312846"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314085"></A><A NAME="_Toc88379425"></A><A NAME="_Toc88379518"></A><A NAME="_Toc88470985"></A><A NAME="_Toc88484595"></A><A NAME="_Toc88484688"></A><A NAME="_Toc88547182"></A><A NAME="_Toc88579428"></A><A NAME="_Toc88580571"></A><A NAME="_Toc88711288"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714045"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt
; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>ARTICLE VIII<BR>
CONDITIONS TO OBLIGATIONS<A NAME="_Toc82881350"></A></B></P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595112"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881266"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881351"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446080"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314086"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944839"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714046"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 8.1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Conditions to Obligations of Buyer</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;The obligation of Buyer to consummate the transactions contemplated by this Agreement is subject to the satisfaction of the following conditions, any one or more of which may be waived in writing by Buyer:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Buyer Approvals shall have been duly made, given or obtained and shall be in full force and effect, and all applicable waiting periods (and any extensions thereof) under the Hart-Scott-Rodino Act shall have expired or otherwise been terminated;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;All of the representations and warranties of Seller contained in this Agreement shall be true and correct in all respects as of the date of this Agreement and as of the Closing, as if made at and as of that time (other than such representations and warranties that expressly address matters only as of a certain date, which need only be true as of such certain date without giving effect to the words &#147;material&#148;, &#147;material adverse effect&#148; or &#147;Material Adverse Effect&#148;, except where the failure to be so true would not, individually or in the aggregate, reasonably be expected to have a Material Adverse Effect on the Companies;</P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Seller shall have performed or complied with all of the covenants and agreements required by this Agreement to be performed or complied with by it at or before the Closing, except where the failure to perform or comply would not reasonably be expected to have a Material Adverse Effect on the Companies;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(d) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Seller shall have delivered to Buyer a certificate from an officer of Seller dated the Closing Date, certifying that the conditions specified in Section 8.1(b) and 8.1(c) have been fulfilled;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(e) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Seller shall have delivered to Buyer a certificate from the Secretary of Seller and from the Secretary of the Companies, each dated as of the Closing Date, attaching and certifying the Organizational Documents and authorizing resolutions of Seller and certifying the incumbency and signatures of the persons signing this Agreement and the other agreements contemplated hereby;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(f) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Seller shall have delivered to Buyer a good standing certificate of recent date for each of the Companies and Seller from their state of organization;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(g) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Seller shall have delivered to Buyer (at least two Business Days before the Closing) a statement containing Seller&#146;s good faith estimate of the Net Working Capital as of the close of business on the Closing Date; and</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(h) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;There shall not be in force any Law, injunction, judgment, order, decree, ruling, or charge restraining or prohibiting the consummation of the transactions contemplated by this Agreement.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595113"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881267"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881352"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446081"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314087"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944841"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714047"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 8.2 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Conditions to the Obligations of Seller</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;The obligation of Seller to consummate the transactions contemplated by this Agreement is subject to the satisfaction of the following conditions, any one or more of which may be waived in writing by Seller:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Seller Approvals shall have been duly made, given or obtained and shall be in full force and effect, and all applicable waiting periods (and any extensions thereof) under the Hart-Scott-Rodino Act shall have expired or otherwise been terminated<FONT COLOR=#0000FF><U>;</U></FONT></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;All of the representations and warranties of Buyer contained in this Agreement shall be true and correct in all respects as of the date of this Agreement and as of the Closing, as if made anew at and as of that time (other than such representations and warranties that expressly address matters only as of a certain date, which need only be true as of such certain date without giving effect to the words &#147;material&#148; or &#147;material adverse effect&#148;, except where the failure to be so true would not, individually or in the aggregate, reasonably be expected to have a material adverse effect on the ability of Buyer to consummate the Closing;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Buyer shall have performed or complied with all of the covenants and agreements required by this Agreement to be performed or complied with by Buyer on or before the Closing, except where the failure to perform or comply would not reasonably be expected to have a Material Adverse Effect;</P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(d) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Buyer shall have delivered to Seller a certificate from an officer of Buyer, dated the Closing Date, certifying that the conditions specified in Section 8.2(b) and 8.2(c) have been fulfilled;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(e) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Buyer shall have delivered to Seller a certificate from the Secretary of Buyer dated as of the Closing Date attaching and certifying the Organizational Documents and authorizing resolutions of Buyer and certifying the incumbency and signatures of the persons signing this Agreement and the other agreements contemplated hereby;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(f) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Buyer shall have delivered to Seller a good standing certificate of recent date for Buyer from its state of organization; and</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(g) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;There shall not be in force any Law, injunction, judgment, order, decree, ruling, or charge restraining or prohibiting the consummation of the transactions contemplated by this Agreement.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc75944843"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595114"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595200"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595289"></A><A NAME="_Toc82844811"></A><A NAME="_Toc82856767"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881268"></A><A NAME="_Toc85445722"></A><A NAME="_Toc85974071"></A><A NAME="_Toc85974384"></A><A NAME="_Toc86037970"></A><A NAME="_Toc86234129"></A><A NAME="_Toc87031686"></A><A NAME="_Toc87106543"></A><A NAME="_Toc87106922"></A><A NAME="_Toc87184110"></A><A NAME="_Toc87365720"></A><A NAME="_Toc87444363"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446082"></A><A NAME="_Toc88122548"></A><A NAME="_Toc88202588"></A><A NAME="_Toc88218715"></A><A NAME="_Toc88219891"></A><A NAME="_Toc88221770"></A><A NAME="_Toc88312849"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314088"></A><A NAME="_Toc88379428"></A><A NAME="_Toc88379521"></A><A NAME="_Toc88470988"></A><A NAME="_Toc88484598"></A><A NAME="_Toc88484691"></A><A NAME="_Toc88547185"></A><A NAME="_Toc88579431"></A><A NAME="_Toc88580574"></A><A NAME="_Toc88711291"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714048"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-
family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>ARTICLE IX<BR>
INDEMNIFICATION<A NAME="_Toc82881353"></A></B></P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595115"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881269"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881354"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446083"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314089"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944845"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714049"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 9.1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Survival</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Subject to Article&nbsp;VII relating to Taxes, all representations and warranties of the Parties contained in this Agreement and all covenants contained in this Agreement that are to be performed prior to the Closing shall survive the Closing until (a) nine months after the Closing Date if the Closing occurs on or prior to December 30, 2004 or (b) 12 months after the Closing Date if the Closing occurs after December 30, 2004, except that the representations and warranties in Section 3.2, 3.5, 3.6, 5.2 and 5.5 shall survive until the fifth anniversary of the Closing Date. &nbsp;No Party shall have any liability for indemnification claims made under this Article&nbsp;IX with respect to any such representation, warranty or covenant unless a Claim Notice is provided by the non-breaching Party to the other Party prior to the expiration of the applicable survival period for such representation, warranty
 or covenant. &nbsp;If a Claim Notice has been timely given in accordance with this Agreement prior to the expiration of the applicable survival period for such representation, warranty or covenant, then the applicable representation, warranty or covenant shall survive as to such claim, until such claim has been finally resolved.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc87446084"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314090"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944847"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595116"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881270"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881355"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714050"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 9.2 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Indemnification.</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to the provisions of this Article&nbsp; IX, from and after the Closing, Seller shall indemnify, defend and hold harmless Buyer, Buyer&#146;s Affiliates (including the Companies from and after the Closing) and their respective Representatives and their respective successors and permitted assigns (the &#147;<B><I>Buyer Indemnified Parties</I></B>&#148;) from and against all Losses that the Buyer Indemnified Parties incur arising from or out of any breach of any representation, warranty or covenant of Seller in this Agreement or in any certificates delivered pursuant to this Agreement; <I>provided, however, </I>that this Section 9.2(a) shall not apply to Section 4.10 or to Article VII.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>For purposes of this Section 9.2(a), each representation and warranty shall be read without giving effect to any materiality or Material Adverse Effect or similar exception or qualifier set forth therein.</P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to the provisions of this Article &nbsp;IX, from and after the Closing, Buyer shall indemnify, defend and hold harmless Seller, the Parent Companies, their respective Affiliates, their respective Representatives and their respective permitted successors and assigns (the &#147;<B><I>Seller Indemnified Parties</I></B>&#148;) from and against all Losses that the Seller Indemnified Parties incur arising from or out of (1) the businesses and operations of the Companies (whether relating to periods prior to or after the Closing Date) to the extent such Losses (A) arise out of a matter for which a Company has liability, (B) are not subject to the provisions of Section 9.2(a) and (C) are not the subject of a Claim Notice delivered by Buyer by the date specified in Section 9.1 or (2) any breach of any representation, 
warranty or covenant of Buyer in this Agreement; <I>provided, however</I>, that this Section 9.2(b) shall not apply to Article VII.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding anything to the contrary herein, the Parties shall have a duty to use Reasonable Efforts to mitigate any Loss arising out of or relating to this Agreement or the transactions contemplated hereby.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(d) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding anything in this Article IX to the contrary, all Losses relating to Taxes which are the subject of Article VII shall only be subject to indemnification under Article VII and the Parent Tax Indemnity Agreement required under Section 2.3(b)(ii).</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595117"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881271"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881356"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446085"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314091"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944849"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714051"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 9.3 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Indemnification Procedures</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Claims for indemnification under this Agreement (other than claims involving a Tax Proceeding, the procedures for which are set forth in Article&nbsp;VII and the Parent Tax Indemnity Agreement required under Section 2.3(b)(ii)) shall be asserted and resolved as follows:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Any Buyer Indemnified Party or Seller Indemnified Party claiming indemnification under this Agreement (an &#147;<B><I>Indemnified Party</I></B>&#148;) with respect to any claim asserted against the Indemnified Party by a third party (&#147;<B><I>Third Party Claim</I></B>&#148;) in respect of any matter that, if true (without any responsibility for independent investigation of the facts or law contained in such notice from the third party), would be subject to indemnification under Section 9.2 shall promptly (i) notify the other Party (the &#147;<B><I>Indemnifying Party</I></B>&#148;) of the Third Party Claim and (ii) transmit to the Indemnifying Party a written notice (&#147;<B><I>Claim Notice</I></B>&#148;) describing in reasonable detail the nature of the Third Party Claim, a copy of all papers served with respect to such claim (if any), th
e Indemnified Party&#146;s best estimate of the amount of Losses attributable to the Third Party Claim and the basis of the Indemnified Party&#146;s request for indemnification under this Agreement. &nbsp;Failure to timely provide such Claim Notice shall not affect the right of the Indemnified Party&#146;s indemnification hereunder, except to the extent the Indemnifying Party is prejudiced by such delay or omission.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Indemnifying Party shall have the right to defend the Indemnified Party against such Third Party Claim. &nbsp;If the Indemnifying Party notifies the Indemnified Party that the Indemnifying Party elects to assume the defense of the Third Party Claim (such election to be without prejudice to the right of the Indemnified Party to dispute whether such claim is an identifiable Loss under this Article&nbsp;IX), then the Indemnifying Party shall have the right to defend such Third Party Claim with counsel selected by the Indemnifying Party (who shall be reasonably satisfactory to the Indemnified Party), by all appropriate proceedings, which proceedings shall be prosecuted diligently by the Indemnifying Party, to a final conclusion or settlement at the discretion of the Indemnifying Party in accordance with this Section 9.3(b). &nbsp;</P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>The Indemnifying Party shall have full control of such defense and proceedings, including any compromise or settlement thereof; <I>provided</I> that the Indemnifying Party shall not enter into any settlement agreement without the written consent of the Indemnified Party (which consent shall not be unreasonably withheld, conditioned or delayed); <I>provided further</I>, that such consent shall not be required if (3) the settlement agreement contains a complete and unconditional general release by the third party asserting the claim to all Indemnified Parties affected by the claim and (4) the settlement agreement does not contain any sanction or restriction upon the conduct of any business by the Indemnified Party or its Affiliates. &nbsp;If requested by the Indemnifying Party, the Indemnified Party agrees, at the sole cost and expense of the Indemnifying Party, t
o cooperate with the Indemnifying Party and its counsel in contesting any Third Party Claim which the Indemnifying Party elects to contest, including the making of any related counterclaim against the Person asserting the Third Party Claim or any cross complaint against any Person. &nbsp;The Indemnified Party may participate in, but not control, any defense or settlement of any Third Party Claim controlled by the Indemnifying Party pursuant to this Section 9.3(b), and the Indemnified Party shall bear its own costs and expenses with respect to such participation.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the Indemnifying Party does not notify the Indemnified Party that the Indemnifying Party elects to defend the Indemnified Party pursuant to Section 9.3(b), then the Indemnified Party shall have the right to defend, and be reimbursed for its reasonable cost and expense (but only if the Indemnified Party is actually entitled to indemnification hereunder) in regard to the Third Party Claim with counsel selected by the Indemnified Party by all appropriate proceedings, which proceedings shall be prosecuted diligently by the Indemnified Party. &nbsp;In such circumstances, the Indemnified Party shall defend any such Third Party Claim in good faith and have full control of such defense and proceedings; <I>provided, however,</I> that the Indemnified Party may not enter into any compromise or settlement of such Third Party Claim if indemnification i
s to be sought hereunder, without the Indemnifying Party&#146;s consent (which consent shall not be unreasonably withheld, conditioned or delayed); <I>provided further</I>, that such consent shall not be required if (i) the settlement agreement contains a complete and unconditional general release by the third party asserting the claim to all Indemnified Parties affected by the claim and (ii) the settlement agreement does not contain any non-monetary obligations of the Indemnifying Party or any sanction or restriction upon the conduct of any business by the Indemnifying Party or its Affiliates. &nbsp;The Indemnifying Party may participate in, but not control, any defense or settlement controlled by the Indemnified Party pursuant to this Section 9.3(c), and the Indemnifying Party shall bear its own costs and expenses with respect to such participation.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(d) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to the other provisions of this &nbsp;Article&nbsp; IX, a claim for indemnification for any matter not involving a Third Party Claim may be asserted by notice to the Party from whom indemnification is sought.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(e) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In the event an Indemnified Party shall recover Losses in respect of a claim of indemnification under this Article IX, no other Indemnified Party shall be entitled to recover the same Losses in respect of a claim for indemnification.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595118"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881272"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881357"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446086"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314092"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944851"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714052"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 9.4 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Limitations on Liability of Seller</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Notwithstanding anything to the contrary herein:</P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;a breach of any representation, warranty or covenant of Seller in this Agreement (other than the representations, warranties and covenants contained in Sections 3.2, 3.5, 3.6 and 4.10 and in Article VII) in connection with any single item or group of related items that results in Losses of less than $100,000 shall be deemed, for all purposes of this Article &nbsp;IX not to be a breach of such representation, warranty<B> </B>or covenant; <I>provided </I>that this limitation shall not apply with respect to any knowing breach by Seller of its covenants in this Agreement;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Seller shall have no liability arising out of or relating to Section 9.2(a) (other than as it applies to Section 3.2, 3.5, 3.6 and 4.17) except if the aggregate Losses actually incurred by the Buyer Indemnified Parties thereunder exceed 2% of the Base Purchase Price (and then, subject to Section 9.4(c), only to the extent such aggregate Losses exceed such amount); <I>provided</I> that this limitation shall not apply with respect to any knowing breach by Seller of its covenants in this Agreement;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;in no event shall Seller&#146;s aggregate liability arising out of or relating to Section 9.2(a) (other than as it applies to Section 3.2 and 3.6) exceed 10% of the Base Purchase Price; <I>provided</I> that this limitation shall not apply with respect to any knowing breach by Seller of its covenants in this Agreement;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(d) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;no Buyer Indemnified Party shall be entitled to indemnification under Section 9.2(a) to the extent Buyer has otherwise been compensated by reasons of adjustments (pursuant to Section 2.4) in the calculation of the Purchase Price relative to what it would have been absent such Loss;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(e) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The amount of any Loss for which a Buyer Indemnified Party claims indemnification under this Agreement shall be reduced by: (i) any third-party insurance proceeds (net of any premiums paid or costs incurred in connection therewith) with respect to such Loss received by the Buyer Indemnified Party; (ii) any net Tax Benefits actually and currently realized with respect to such Loss and (iii) indemnification or reimbursement payments received from third parties with respect to such Loss (it being agreed that Buyer shall use Reasonable Efforts to obtain any such amounts described in clauses (i), (ii) and (iii) that may be available); and</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(f) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Seller shall have no liability for any breach of a representation or warranty in this Agreement by Seller of which Buyer had Knowledge on or prior to the date of this Agreement.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc87446087"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314093"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944857"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595120"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881274"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881359"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714053"></A><BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 9.5 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Waiver of Other Representations.</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;NOTWITHSTANDING ANYTHING TO THE CONTRARY HEREIN, IT IS THE EXPLICIT INTENT OF EACH PARTY HERETO, AND THE PARTIES HEREBY AGREE, THAT NONE OF SELLER, ENTERGY, KOCH OR ANY OF THEIR RESPECTIVE AFFILIATES OR REPRESENTATIVES HAS MADE OR IS MAKING ANY REPRESENTATION OR WARRANTY WHATSOEVER, EXPRESS OR IMPLIED, WRITTEN OR ORAL, INCLUDING ANY IMPLIED REPRESENTATION OR WARRANTY AS TO THE CONDITION, MERCHANTABILITY, USAGE, SUITABILITY OR FITNESS FOR ANY PARTICULAR PURPOSE WITH RESPECT TO THE PURCHASED INTERESTS, THE COMPANIES, THEIR ASSETS, OR ANY PART THEREOF, EXCEPT THOSE REPRESENTATIONS AND WARRANTIES CONTAINED IN THIS AGREEMENT, AND WITHOUT IN ANY WAY LIMITING THE FOREGOING, SELLER MAKES NO REPRESENTATION OR WARRANTY TO BUYER WITH RESPECT TO ANY FINANCIAL PROJECTIONS OR FORECASTS RELATING TO THE COMPANIES.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;EXCEPT AS OTHERWISE EXPRESSLY PROVIDED HEREIN, SELLER&#146;S INTERESTS IN THE COMPANIES AND THEIR ASSETS ARE BEING TRANSFERRED THROUGH THE SALE OF THE PURCHASED INTERESTS &#147;AS IS, WHERE IS, WITH ALL FAULTS,&#148; AND SELLER EXPRESSLY DISCLAIMS ANY REPRESENTATIONS OR WARRANTIES OF ANY KIND OR NATURE, EXPRESS OR IMPLIED, AS TO THE CONDITION, VALUE OR QUALITY OF THE COMPANIES AND THEIR ASSETS OR THE PROSPECTS (FINANCIAL OR OTHERWISE), RISKS AND OTHER INCIDENTS OF THE COMPANIES AND THEIR ASSETS.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The representations and warranties contained in Section 4.11 shall be the exclusive representations and warranties with regard to Environmental Laws and related matters.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595121"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881275"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881360"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446088"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314094"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944859"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714054"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 9.6 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Purchase Price Adjustment</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;The Parties agree to treat all payments made pursuant to this Article IX as adjustments to the Purchase Price for Tax purposes.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595119"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881273"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881358"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446089"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314095"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714055"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 9.7 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Exclusive Remedy</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding anything to the contrary herein, except as provided (i) in Section 2.1, 2.2, and 2.3 (as to all of which Buyer shall be entitled to specific performance and Seller shall be entitled to damages without regard to the limitations provided in Section 9.7(c) below), (ii)&nbsp;in Section 6.6(b), 6.8(c), 7.1, 7.2, 7.3, 7.4, 9.2 or 10.2, (iii)&nbsp;in the Parent Tax Indemnity Agreement required under Section 2.3(b)(ii) or (iv)&nbsp;in the case of fraud, no Party shall have any liability, and no Party shall make any claim, for any Loss or other matter (and Buyer and Seller hereby waive any right of contribution against the other, the Parent Companies, and their respective Affiliates), under, arising out of or relating to this Agreement, any other document, agreement, certificate or other matter delivered pursuant hereto or the transact
ions contemplated hereby, whether based on contract, tort, strict liability, other Laws or otherwise.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;With respect to any Third Party Claim brought against Seller (whether such claim or demand is pursuant to this Agreement, applicable law or otherwise), Seller hereby agrees on its own behalf and on behalf of Koch, Entergy, and their respective Affiliates that it </P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>and they will not make any claim for (i)&nbsp;indemnification against the Companies by reason solely of the fact that they (or any of their Affiliates) were a member, general partner, limited partner or agent of the Companies or were serving at the request of the Companies as a partner, member, trustee, or agent of another entity (whether such claim is for judgments, damages, penalties, fines, costs, amounts paid in settlement, losses, expenses, or otherwise and whether such claim is pursuant to any statute, organizational document agreement or otherwise) or (ii)&nbsp;contribution against the Companies by reason solely of the fact that the Companies were a party to any action or inaction that forms the basis of such claim or demand. </P>
<A NAME="_Toc75944861"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595122"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595208"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595297"></A><A NAME="_Toc82844819"></A><A NAME="_Toc82856775"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881276"></A><A NAME="_Toc85445730"></A><A NAME="_Toc85974079"></A><A NAME="_Toc85974392"></A><A NAME="_Toc86037978"></A><A NAME="_Toc86234137"></A><A NAME="_Toc87031694"></A><A NAME="_Toc87106551"></A><A NAME="_Toc87106930"></A><A NAME="_Toc87184118"></A><A NAME="_Toc87365728"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;NOTWITHSTANDING ANYTHING TO THE CONTRARY HEREIN (OTHER THAN SECTION 9.7(a) NO PARTY SHALL BE LIABLE FOR SPECIAL, PUNITIVE, EXEMPLARY, INCIDENTAL, CONSEQUENTIAL OR INDIRECT DAMAGES, LOST PROFITS OR LOST BENEFITS, LOSS OF ENTERPRISE VALUE, DIMINUTION IN VALUE OF ANY BUSINESS, DAMAGE TO REPUTATION OR LOSS TO GOODWILL, WHETHER BASED ON CONTRACT, TORT, STRICT LIABILITY, OTHER LAW OR OTHERWISE AND 
WHETHER OR NOT ARISING FROM ANY OTHER PARTY&#146;S SOLE, JOINT OR CONCURRENT NEGLIGENCE, STRICT LIABILITY OR OTHER FAULT; <I>PROVIDED, HOWEVER, </I>THAT THIS SECTION 9.7(c) SHALL NOT LIMIT A PARTY&#146;S RIGHT TO RECOVERY UNDER ARTICLE IX FOR ANY SUCH DAMAGES TO THE EXTENT SUCH PARTY IS REQUIRED TO PAY SUCH DAMAGES TO A THIRD PARTY IN CONNECTION WITH A MATTER FOR WHICH SUCH PARTY IS OTHERWISE ENTITLED TO INDEMNIFICATION UNDER ARTICLE IX.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc87444371"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446090"></A><A NAME="_Toc88122556"></A><A NAME="_Toc88202596"></A><A NAME="_Toc88218723"></A><A NAME="_Toc88219899"></A><A NAME="_Toc88221778"></A><A NAME="_Toc88312857"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314096"></A><A NAME="_Toc88379436"></A><A NAME="_Toc88379529"></A><A NAME="_Toc88470996"></A><A NAME="_Toc88484606"></A><A NAME="_Toc88484699"></A><A NAME="_Toc88547193"></A><A NAME="_Toc88579439"></A><A NAME="_Toc88580582"></A><A NAME="_Toc88711299"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714056"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>ARTICLE X<BR>
TERMINATION<A NAME="_Toc82881361"></A></B></P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595123"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881277"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881362"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446091"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314097"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944863"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714057"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 10.1 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Termination</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;At any time prior to the Closing, this Agreement may be terminated and the transactions contemplated hereby abandoned:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;by the mutual consent of Buyer and Seller as evidenced in writing signed by each of Buyer and Seller;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;by Buyer, if there has been a material breach by Seller of any representation, warranty or covenant contained in this Agreement which has prevented the satisfaction of any condition to the obligations of Buyer at the Closing and, if such breach is of a character that it is capable of being cured, such breach has not been cured by Seller within 30 days after written notice thereof from Buyer;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;by Seller, if there has been a material breach by Buyer of any representation, warranty or covenant contained in this Agreement which has prevented the satisfaction of any condition to the obligations of Seller at the Closing and, if such breach is of a character that it is capable of being cured, such breach has not been cured by Buyer within 30 days after written notice thereof from Seller;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(d) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;by either Buyer or Seller if any Governmental Authority having competent jurisdiction has issued a final, non-appealable order, decree, ruling or injunction (other than a </P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>temporary restraining order) or taken any other action permanently restraining, enjoining or otherwise prohibiting the transactions contemplated by this Agreement; or</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(e) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;by either Buyer or Seller, if the Closing has not occurred on or before March 31, 2005, or such later date as the Parties may agree upon.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595124"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881278"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881363"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446092"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314098"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944865"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714058"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 10.2 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Effect of Termination</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;In the event of termination and abandonment of this Agreement pursuant to Section 10.1, this Agreement shall forthwith become void and have no effect, without any liability on the part of any Party hereto; <I>provided, however, </I>that if this Agreement is validly terminated by a Party as a result of an intentional, material breach of this Agreement by the non-terminating Party, then the terminating Party shall be entitled to all rights and remedies available under Law or equity. &nbsp;The provisions of Sections 6.6(b) (the fifth sentence only), 11.4 and 11.12 hereof shall survive any termination of this Agreement. &nbsp;The Confidentiality Agreement shall not be affected by a termination of this Agreement.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc75944867"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595125"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595211"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595300"></A><A NAME="_Toc82844822"></A><A NAME="_Toc82856778"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881279"></A><A NAME="_Toc83613073"></A><A NAME="_Toc85445733"></A><A NAME="_Toc85974082"></A><A NAME="_Toc85974395"></A><A NAME="_Toc86037981"></A><A NAME="_Toc86234140"></A><A NAME="_Toc87031697"></A><A NAME="_Toc87106554"></A><A NAME="_Toc87106933"></A><A NAME="_Toc87184121"></A><A NAME="_Toc87365731"></A><A NAME="_Toc87444374"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446093"></A><A NAME="_Toc88122559"></A><A NAME="_Toc88202599"></A><A NAME="_Toc88218726"></A><A NAME="_Toc88219902"></A><A NAME="_Toc88221781"></A><A NAME="_Toc88312860"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314099"></A><A NAME="_Toc88379439"></A><A NAME="_Toc88379532"></A><A NAME="_Toc88470999"></A><A NAME="_Toc88484609"></A><A NAME="_Toc88484702"></A><A NAME="_Toc88547196"></A><A NAME="_Toc88579442"></A><A NAME="_Toc88580585"></A><A NAME="_Toc88711302"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714059"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt

<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;No Party shall assign this Agreement or any part hereof without the prior written consent of the other Party; <I>provided, however, </I>that Buyer may (i)&nbsp;assign any or all of its rights and interests hereunder to one or more of its Affiliates and (ii)&nbsp;designate one or more of its Affiliates to perform its obligations hereunder as long as (A)&nbsp;Buyer remains responsible for the performance of all of its obligations hereunder), (B) Loews Corporation remains responsible for its obligations under the Parent Guaranty of even date herewith from it to Seller and (C)&nbsp;such assignment or designation would not cause a delay in obtaining the Buyer Approvals or the Seller Approvals or require any other approvals. &nbsp;Subject to the foregoing, this Agreement shall be binding upon and inure to the benefit of the Parties and their respective permitted successors and assigns.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595128"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881282"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881367"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446096"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314102"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944873"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714062"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 11.3 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Rights of Third Parties</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Except for the provisions of Section 9.2 which are intended to be enforceable by the Persons respectively referred to therein, nothing expressed or implied in this Agreement is intended or shall be construed to confer upon or give any Person, other than the Parties, any right or remedies under or by reason of this Agreement.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595129"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881283"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881368"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446097"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314103"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944875"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714063"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 11.4 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Expenses</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Except as otherwise provided herein, each Party shall bear its own expenses incurred in connection with this Agreement and the transactions herein contemplated hereby whether or not such transactions shall be consummated, including all fees of its legal counsel, financial advisers and accountants; provided that all out-of-pocket fees, costs and expenses incurred by the Companies in connection with this Agreement prior to Closing and not reflected in the Net Working Capital calculation shall be the sole obligations of Seller and shall be paid by Seller without reimbursement from the Companies.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc75944877"></A><A NAME="_Toc82595130"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881284"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881369"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446098"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314104"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714064"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 11.5 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Counterparts</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;This Agreement may be executed in two or more counterparts, each of which shall be deemed an original, but all of which together shall constitute one and the same instrument. &nbsp;Any facsimile copies hereof or signature hereon shall, for all purposes, be deemed originals.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595131"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881285"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881370"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446099"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314105"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944879"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714065"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 11.6 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Entire Agreement</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;This Agreement (together with the Disclosure Schedule and exhibits to this Agreement) and the Confidentiality Agreement constitute the entire </P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>agreement among the Parties and supersede any other agreements, whether written or oral, that may have been made or entered into by or among any of the Parties or any of their respective Affiliates relating to the transactions contemplated hereby. &nbsp;No representations, warranties, covenants, understandings or agreements, oral or otherwise, relating to the transactions contemplated by this Agreement exist between Buyer, on the one hand, and, Seller, Koch, Entergy or any of their respective Affiliates, on the other hand, except as expressly set forth in this Agreement and the Confidentiality Agreement.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595132"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881286"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881371"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446100"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314106"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944883"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714066"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 11.7 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Disclosure Schedule</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Unless the context otherwise requires, all capitalized terms used in the Disclosure Schedule shall have the respective meanings assigned in this Agreement. &nbsp;No reference to or disclosure of any item or other matter in the Disclosure Schedule shall be construed as an admission or indication that such item or other matter is material or that such item or other matter is required to be referred to or disclosed in the Disclosure Schedule. &nbsp;No disclosure in the Disclosure Schedule relating to any possible breach or violation of any agreement or Law shall be construed as an admission or indication that any such breach or violation exists or has actually occurred. The inclusion of any information in the Disclosure Schedule shall not be deemed to be an admission or acknowledgment by Seller, in and of itself, that such information is material to or outside the ordinary course of the business of t
he Companies or required to be disclosed on the Disclosure Schedule. &nbsp;Each disclosure in the Disclosure Schedule shall constitute disclosure for purposes of the corresponding Sections or subsections of this Agreement expressly referred to in the Disclosure Schedule and any other Section or subsection to the extent such disclosure is made in such a way as to make its relevance to such other Section or subsection readily apparent. &nbsp;</P>
<A NAME="_Toc87446101"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314107"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714067"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 11.8 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Acknowledgment by Buyer</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;Buyer has not relied on any representation or warranty from Seller, Entergy, Koch or any of their respective Affiliates, except as set forth in this Agreement.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595133"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881287"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881372"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446102"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314108"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944885"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714068"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 11.9 &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B><I>Amendments</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;This Agreement may be amended or modified in whole or in part, and terms and conditions may be waived, only by a duly authorized agreement in writing which makes reference to this Agreement executed by each Party.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595134"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881288"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881373"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446103"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314109"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944887"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714069"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 11.10 &nbsp;<B><I>Publicity</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;All press releases or other public communications of any nature whatsoever relating to the transactions contemplated by this Agreement, and the method of the release for publication thereof, shall be subject to the prior written consent of Buyer and Seller, which consent shall not be unreasonably withheld, conditioned or delayed by any Party; <I>provided, however,</I> that nothing herein shall prevent a Party from publishing such press releases or other public communications as such Party may consider necessary in order to satisfy such Party&#146;s obligations at Law or under the rules of any stock or commodities exchange after consultation with the other Party as is reasonable under the circumstances.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595135"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881289"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881374"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446104"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314110"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944889"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714070"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 11.11 &nbsp;<B><I>Severability</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>. &nbsp;If any provision of this Agreement is held invalid or unenforceable by any court of competent jurisdiction, the other provisions of this Agreement shall remain in full force and effect. &nbsp;The Parties further agree that if any provision contained herein is, to any extent, held invalid or unenforceable in any respect under the Laws governing this Agreement, they shall take any actions necessary to render the remaining provisions of this Agreement valid and enforceable to the fullest extent permitted by Law and, to the extent </P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>necessary, shall amend or otherwise modify this Agreement to replace any provision contained herein that is held invalid or unenforceable with a valid and enforceable provision giving effect to the intent of the Parties to the greatest extent legally permissible.</P>
<A NAME="_Toc82595136"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881290"></A><A NAME="_Toc82881375"></A><A NAME="_Toc87446105"></A><A NAME="_Toc88314111"></A><A NAME="_Toc75944891"></A><A NAME="_Toc88714071"></A><P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times; font-size:12pt" align=justify>Section 11.12 &nbsp;<B><I>Governing Law; Jurisdiction. &nbsp;</I></B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(a) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This Agreement shall be governed and construed in accordance with the Laws of the State of New York without regard to the Laws that might be applicable under conflicts of laws principles other than Section 5-1401 of the New York General Obligations Law.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(b) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Parties agree that the appropriate, exclusive and convenient forum for any disputes between any of the Parties hereto arising out of this Agreement or the transactions contemplated hereby shall be in any state or federal court in Wilmington, Delaware, and each of the Parties hereto irrevocably submits to the jurisdiction of such courts solely in respect of any legal proceeding arising out of or related to this Agreement. &nbsp;The Parties further agree that the Parties shall not bring suit with respect to any disputes arising out of this Agreement or the transactions contemplated hereby in any court or jurisdiction other than the above specified courts; <I>provided, however,</I> that the foregoing shall not limit the rights of the Parties to obtain execution of judgment in any other jurisdiction. &nbsp;The Parties further agree, to the ex
tent permitted by Law, that a final and unappealable judgment against a Party in any action or proceeding contemplated above shall be conclusive and may be enforced in any other jurisdiction within or outside the United States by suit on the judgment, a certified or exemplified copy of which shall be conclusive evidence of the fact and amount of such judgment. &nbsp;Except to the extent that a different determination or finding is mandated due to the applicable law being that of a different jurisdiction, the Parties agree that all judicial determinations or findings by a state or federal court in Wilmington, Delaware with respect to any matter under this Agreement shall be binding.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(c) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;To the extent that any Party hereto has or hereafter may acquire any immunity from jurisdiction of any court or from any legal process (whether through service or notice, attachment prior to judgment, attachment in aid of execution, execution or otherwise) with respect to itself or its property, each such party hereby irrevocably (i) waives such immunity in respect of its obligations with respect to this Agreement and (ii) submits to the personal jurisdiction of any court described in Section 11.12(b).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:72pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>(d) &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;THE PARTIES HERETO AGREE THAT THEY HEREBY IRREVOCABLY WAIVE THE RIGHT TO TRIAL BY JURY IN ANY ACTION TO ENFORCE OR INTERPRET THE PROVISIONS OF THIS AGREEMENT.</P>
<BR>

<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>SELLER</B>:</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>ENTERGY-KOCH, LP</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>By</B>: &nbsp;<B>EKLP, LLC, its General Partner</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>By</B>: &nbsp;<B>EK Holding III, LLC, its Manager</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;By: &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</U></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Name: &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</U></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Title: &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</U></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>BUYER</B>:</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<B>TGT PIPELINE, LLC</B></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><BR></P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;By: &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Name: &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Title: &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>Exhibit 2.3(b)(i)</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=center><B>Form of Assignment and Assumption Agreement</B></P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>This ASSIGNMENT AND ASSUMPTION AGREEMENT, dated as of ___________ (this &#147;<B><I>Assignment</I></B>&#148;), is entered into by and between Entergy-Koch, LP, a limited partnership organized under the Laws of Delaware (&#147;<B><I>Seller</I></B>&#148;), and TGT Pipeline, LLC, a limited liability company organized under the Laws of Delaware (&#147;<B><I>Buyer</I></B>&#148;).</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>WHEREAS, Seller owns (i) 100% of the member interests in GS Pipeline Company, LLC, a limited liability company organized under the Laws of Delaware (&#147;<B><I>GS Pipeline</I></B>&#148;), which is the owner of 100% of the general partner interests in Gulf South Pipeline Company, LP, a limited partnership organized under the Laws of Delaware (&#147;<B><I>Gulf South</I></B>&#148;) and (ii)&nbsp;100% of the limited partner interests in Gulf South (such member interests in GS Pipeline and limited partner interests in Gulf South being collectively the &#147;<B><I>Purchased Interests</I></B>&#148;);</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>WHEREAS, Seller and Buyer have entered into that certain Purchase and Sale Agreement dated as of November__, 2004 (the &#147;<B><I>PSA</I></B>&#148;), providing, among other things, for the sale by Seller and the purchase by Buyer of the Purchased Interests; and</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>WHEREAS, pursuant to the PSA, Seller and Buyer are required to execute and deliver this Assignment to effect the transfer by Seller to Buyer of the Purchased Interests;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the mutual covenants contained herein and in the PSA and other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and sufficiency of which are hereby acknowledged, Seller and Buyer covenant and agree as follows:</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B><I>1. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Defined Terms.</I></B> &nbsp;All capitalized terms used but not defined herein shall have the meanings set forth for such terms in the PSA.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B><I>2. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Assignment</I></B><I>.</I> &nbsp;Seller has granted, conveyed, sold, assigned, transferred, bargained and delivered, and hereby, grants, conveys, sells, assigns, transfers, bargains and delivers free and clear of all Liens (other than transfer restrictions imposed thereon by applicable securities Laws), unto Buyer and its successors and assigns and Buyer hereby accepts, purchases and acquires Seller&#146;s right, title and interest in and to the Purchased Interests.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify>TO HAVE AND TO HOLD the Purchased Interests unto Buyer and its successors and assigns forever.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B><I>3. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Assumption.</I></B> &nbsp;Buyer agrees to assume and fully perform, and indemnifies Seller against all liabilities relating to, all of Seller&#146;s obligations and liabilities under and in respect of the Purchased Interests.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B><I>4. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Disclaimer of Warranties.</I></B> &nbsp;Except to the extent expressly set forth in the PSA, Seller does not make any representation or warranty whatsoever (orally or in writing) to Buyer. &nbsp;Except as provided in the PSA, the Purchased Interests are being transferred &#147;as is, where is, with all faults&#148; and Seller expressly disclaims any representations or warranties of any kind or nature, express or implied, as to the Purchased Interests.</P>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<BR>
<P style="page-break-before:always; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B><I>5. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Withdrawal; Admission.</I></B> &nbsp;Effective as of the date hereof, (a) Seller hereby withdraws as the sole limited partner of Gulf South and Buyer is hereby admitted as the sole limited partner of Gulf South and (b) Seller hereby withdraws as the sole member of GS Pipeline and Buyer is hereby admitted as the sole member of GS Pipeline.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B><I>6. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Further Assurances.</I></B> &nbsp;Seller and Buyer agree to execute, acknowledge and deliver all such further documents and to do such further acts as are or may be reasonably necessary or appropriate more fully to carry out the intent of this Assignment.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B><I>7. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Conflict and Inconsistency; No Merger.</I></B> &nbsp;The terms and provisions of the PSA (including, without limitation, the representations, warranties and covenants therein) shall not merge, be extinguished or otherwise affected by the delivery and execution of this Assignment or any other document delivered pursuant to this Assignment and in the event of conflict the terms of the PSA shall prevail.</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B><I>8. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Governing Law.</I></B> &nbsp;This Assignment shall be governed by, and construed in accordance with, the Laws of the State of New York, without regard to the Laws that might be applicable under conflicts of laws principles, other than Section 5-1401 of the New York General Obligations Law. </P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B><I>9. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Binding Effect.</I></B> &nbsp;This Assignment shall be binding upon and shall inure to the benefit of the parties hereto and their respective successors and assigns. &nbsp;</P>
<P style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:12pt; text-indent:36pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:12pt" align=justify><B><I>10. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Counterparts.</I></B> &nbsp;This Assignment may be executed in one or more counterparts, each of which shall be deemed an original, but all of which shall constitute one and the same instrument.</P>
